Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-28 05:53:16]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = 1002

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details:

[2018-11-28 06:00:18]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT id,name FROM cms_clients WHERE is_active = 1


[2018-11-28 06:00:18]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-28 06:45:41]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details:

[2018-11-28 07:04:06]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, leaving_reason

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-11-28 22:03:59]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

						  outbound_no		
						, date_format(outbound_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as outbound_date

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-28 23:00:19]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-28 23:10:14]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10
